Overview  

![Collapse](https://profiles.viictr.org/Profile/Modules/PropertyList/images/minusSign.gif)
overview

Clinical Interests  
  
Barrett's esophagus, gastroesophageal reflux disease (GERD), dyspepsia,
irritable bowel syndrome (IBS), celiac disease, colonoscopy,
esophagogastroduodenoscopy (EGD), bravo pH monitoring, chronic liver disease,
and liver cancer
